DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV NODE_VERSION=18.17.1
  ENV DENO_VERSION=1.42.3
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  # Set working directory to the repository root as per plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  # Install core dependencies: curl, git, python3, build tools, ulimit tools, and browsers
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      python3 python3-distutils python3-venv python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      software-properties-common \
      gnupg2 \
      unzip \
      wget \
      xz-utils \
      locales \
      bash-completion \
      dumb-init \
      procps \
      ulimit \
      fontconfig \
      # Install Chromium browser (for Chrome extension testing)
      chromium-browser \
      # Install Firefox ESR (>=78)
      firefox-esr \
      # Install Thunderbird (>=78.0a1)
      thunderbird \
      # Install yarn dependencies for completeness
      npm \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Generate locale to avoid locale warnings
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Install Node.js 18.x (latest LTS) from official NodeSource binaries
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g npm@latest \
      && npm install -g typescript ts-node yarn \
      && node -v \
      && npm -v \
      && tsc -v \
      && ts-node --version \
      && yarn --version
  # Install Deno latest stable for Linux x86_64
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deno.land/install.sh | DENO_INSTALL=/usr/local deno_install.sh \
      && ln -s /usr/local/bin/deno /usr/bin/deno \
      && deno --version
  # Increase open files limit for the container (ulimit)
  RUN echo "fs.file-max = 65535" >> /etc/sysctl.conf \
      && ulimit -n 65535 || true
  # Copy repository contents into container
  # Assuming build context is root of repo, copy all files
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  # Set permissions and ownership for copied files (ensure all files are accessible)
  RUN chown -R root:root /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader \
      && chmod -R u+rwX /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  # Prepare npm dependencies: clean install with npm ci, no legacy peer deps
  RUN npm ci --max-old-space-size=4096
  # Expose environment variables for node to leverage max memory during builds and ESM support
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max-old-space-size=4096"
  # Default shell environment with bash and working directory set
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  # Entrypoint to bash shell with dumb-init for signal handling
  ENTRYPOINT ["dumb-init", "--"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV NODE_VERSION=18.17.1
  ENV DENO_VERSION=1.42.3
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      python3 python3-distutils python3-venv python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      software-properties-common \
      gnupg2 \
      unzip \
      wget \
      xz-utils \
      locales \
      bash-completion \
      dumb-init \
      procps \
      fontconfig \
      chromium \
      firefox \
      thunderbird \
      npm \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g npm@latest \
      && npm install -g typescript ts-node yarn \
      && node -v \
      && npm -v \
      && tsc -v \
      && ts-node --version \
      && yarn --version
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deno.land/install.sh | DENO_INSTALL=/usr/local deno_install.sh \
      && ln -s /usr/local/bin/deno /usr/bin/deno \
      && deno --version
  RUN echo "fs.file-max = 65535" >> /etc/sysctl.conf \
      && ulimit -n 65535 || true
  COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  RUN chown -R root:root /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader \
      && chmod -R u+rwX /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  RUN npm ci --max-old-space-size=4096
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max-old-space-size=4096"
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/darkreader_darkreader
  ENTRYPOINT ["dumb-init", "--"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV NODE_VERSION=18.17.1
  ENV DENO_VERSION=1.42.3
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      python3 python3-distutils python3-venv python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      software-properties-common \
      gnupg2 \
      unzip \
      wget \
      xz-utils \
      locales \
      bash-completion \
      dumb-init \
      procps \
      fontconfig \
      chromium-browser \
      firefox \
      thunderbird \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x | bash -
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y nodejs
  RUN npm install -g npm@latest
  RUN npm install -g typescript
  RUN npm install -g ts-node
  RUN npm install -g yarn
  RUN node -v
  RUN npm -v
  RUN tsc -v
  RUN ts-node --version
  RUN yarn --version
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deno.land/install.sh | DENO_INSTALL=/usr/local sh
  RUN ln -s /usr/local/bin/deno /usr/bin/deno
  RUN deno --version
  RUN echo "fs.file-max = 65535" >> /etc/sysctl.conf \
      && ulimit -n 65535 || true
  COPY . /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN chown -R root:root /darkreader_darkreader \
      && chmod -R u+rwX /darkreader_darkreader
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN npm ci --max-old-space-size=4096
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max-old-space-size=4096"
  ENTRYPOINT ["dumb-init", "--"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV NODE_VERSION=18.17.1
  ENV DENO_VERSION=1.42.3
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      python3 python3-distutils python3-venv python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      software-properties-common \
      gnupg2 \
      unzip \
      wget \
      xz-utils \
      locales \
      bash-completion \
      dumb-init \
      procps \
      fontconfig \
      chromium-browser \
      firefox \
      thunderbird \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x | bash - && \
      apt-get update && apt-get install -y nodejs && \
      node -v && npm -v && \
      npm install -g --unsafe-perm=true npm@latest typescript ts-node yarn && \
      npm -v && tsc -v && ts-node --version && yarn --version
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deno.land/install.sh | DENO_INSTALL=/usr/local sh
  RUN ln -s /usr/local/bin/deno /usr/bin/deno
  RUN deno --version
  RUN echo "fs.file-max = 65535" >> /etc/sysctl.conf \
      && ulimit -n 65535 || true
  COPY . /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN chown -R root:root /darkreader_darkreader \
      && chmod -R u+rwX /darkreader_darkreader
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN npm ci --max-old-space-size=4096
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max-old-space-size=4096"
  ENTRYPOINT ["dumb-init", "--"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV NODE_VERSION=18.17.1
  ENV DENO_VERSION=1.42.3
  ENV PYTHON_VERSION=3.10
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      python3 python3-distutils python3-venv python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      software-properties-common \
      gnupg2 \
      unzip \
      wget \
      xz-utils \
      locales \
      bash-completion \
      dumb-init \
      procps \
      fontconfig \
      chromium-browser \
      firefox \
      thunderbird \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x -o nodesource_setup.sh && \
      bash nodesource_setup.sh && \
      rm nodesource_setup.sh
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y nodejs && \
      node -v && npm -v
  RUN npm cache clean --force && \
      npm install -g --unsafe-perm=true npm@latest && \
      npm -v
  RUN npm install -g typescript && tsc -v
  RUN npm install -g ts-node && ts-node --version
  RUN npm install -g yarn && yarn --version
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deno.land/install.sh | DENO_INSTALL=/usr/local sh
  RUN ln -s /usr/local/bin/deno /usr/bin/deno
  RUN deno --version
  RUN echo "fs.file-max = 65535" >> /etc/sysctl.conf \
      && ulimit -n 65535 || true
  COPY . /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN chown -R root:root /darkreader_darkreader \
      && chmod -R u+rwX /darkreader_darkreader
  WORKDIR /darkreader_darkreader
  RUN npm ci --max-old-space-size=4096
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max-old-space-size=4096"
  ENTRYPOINT ["dumb-init", "--"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
